Constitution Day: Date: 26 November 2024
Description: Constitution Day was celebrated on 26 November 2024 to honour the adoption of the Indian Constitution 
and promote awareness of the democratic values and principles enshrined within it. As part of the observance, students 
and faculty came together to read the Preamble to the Constitution, reaffirming their dedication to justice, liberty, 
equality, and fraternity. A special highlight of the event was a thematic skit performed by students on the life and legacy 
of Bhagwan Birsa Munda, a revered tribal freedom fighter. The performance effectively connected his struggle for rights 
and justice with the core values upheld by the Indian Constitution, emphasizing the enduring relevance of his 
contributions in the context of constitutional awareness. EBSB members played an instrumental role in organizing the 
activities, fostering a spirit of unity, awareness, and respect for the Constitution and India’s rich tribal heritage.
Yuva Sangam Phase 5 – West Bengal Visit: Date: 02 December – 11 December 2024
As a premier institute of national importance, IIT Jodhpur takes immense pride in being the host and facilitator of Yuva 
Sangam Phase-V under the EBSB initiative. With a steadfast commitment to fostering cultural and academic exchanges, 
IIT Jodhpur provided a dynamic platform for youth from Rajasthan and West Bengal to connect, collaborate, and 
celebrate India’s rich diversity.
To ensure meaningful participation, IIT Jodhpur organized a series of screening rounds to carefully select enthusiastic and 
deserving students from Rajasthan. Once selected, arrangements were made for their comfortable stay on the IIT Jodhpur 
campus prior to their departure to IIEST, Shibpur (West Bengal) as part of the exchange.
The journey commenced with a flag-off ceremony at IIT Jodhpur, graced by the presence of our Hon’ble Director, IIT 
Jodhpur, and Shri Naveen Ji from AICTE. As a gesture of unity, identity, and preparedness, all participating students 
from Rajasthan were provided with high-quality merchandise including uppers, caps, and ID badges, symbolizing their 
role as cultural ambassadors of the state.
Throughout the program, IIT Jodhpur ensured seamless execution of all activities, creating a welcoming and enriching 
environment for the participants. Although time constraints limited the extent of local exploration, the essence of 
Rajasthan’s vibrant culture and progressive spirit was meaningfully shared with the visiting delegates.
IIT Jodhpur remains deeply committed to promoting national unity through such transformative initiatives, reaffirming 
its role as a leading institution that bridges academic excellence with cultural heritage. We look forward to contributing 
actively to future editions of Yuva Sangam, furthering the vision of EBSB through continued collaboration, engagement, 
and shared learning.
Yuva Sangam Phase 5 – Hosting West Bengal Delegates: Date: 13 December – 19 December 2024
Description: IIT Jodhpur proudly hosted Yuva Sangam Phase V, a flagship initiative under EBSB, in collaboration with 
Indian Institute of Engineering Science and Technology, Shibpur (IIEST Shibpur). This phase focused on a cultural and 
academic exchange between the youth of Rajasthan and West Bengal, aiming to foster mutual understanding, respect, and 
national integration.
As part of the program, a delegation of 40 students from West Bengal visited Rajasthan from 14th to 18th December 2024. 
The visit was thoughtfully planned to provide a holistic exposure to Rajasthan’s historical richness, cultural vibrancy, and 
academic environment.
The key activities conducted during the exchange included:
•
Campus Visit and Welcome at IIT Jodhpur, including interaction with faculty, students, and dignitaries.
•
Visits to prominent heritage sites such as Mehrangarh Fort, Ghanta Ghar, and Toorji Ka Jhalra, offering firsthand
insight into Rajasthan’s architectural grandeur and history.
•
Engagement with Rajasthani traditions, including local cuisine tasting and a special lecture on Rajasthan’s history
and heritage by historian Rajveer Chalkoi.
•
Village exposure visits to Salawas and Osian, where students interacted with local communities and witnessed rural
lifestyles and crafts.
•
Royal interaction with H.H. Maharaja Shri Gaj Singh II of Jodhpur, providing valuable perspectives on Rajasthan’s
royal heritage and governance.
•
Cultural immersion through a workshop on Rajasthani folk dance and music, encouraging hands-on learning of
regional art forms.
•
Cultural evening featuring performances by delegates from West Bengal, including a skit based on Gurudev
Rabindranath Tagore’s "Beer Purush", followed by a valedictory ceremony.
This enriching program not only highlighted the cultural similarities and differences between the two states but also 
reinforced the values of unity in diversity. The Yuva Sangam initiative served as a platform for youth to develop mutual 
respect, national pride, and lifelong connections beyond regional boundaries.

Republic Day: Date: 26 January 2025
Description: IIT Jodhpur celebrated the 76th Republic Day on 26th January 2025 with great patriotism and enthusiasm. The 
event honoured the adoption of the Indian Constitution and the democratic values that form the foundation of the nation.
The celebrations began with a flag hoisting ceremony, followed by a parade, patriotic songs, and inspiring speeches 
reflecting on India's journey as a sovereign democratic republic. As part of the cultural segment, members of the EBSB 
student team made a special contribution by performing a patriotic group song, adding a soulful and emotional dimension 
to the event. Their performance captured the spirit of unity, cultural pride, and love for the nation, resonating strongly 
with the audience.
Virasat: Date: 13 February – 17 February 2025
Description: Virasat, a prestigious cultural heritage festival organized under the banner of SPIC MACAY, was held at IIT 
Jodhpur from 13th to 17th February 2025. The festival celebrated the richness of Indian classical music, dance, traditional 
crafts, and art forms, offering the IITJ community and visitors a profound cultural experience rooted in India’s heritage. As 
part of the organizing support team, the EBSB student members played a crucial and commendable role throughout the 
event. Their key contributions included:
•
Coordinating pick-up and drop facilities for all participating artists and guests from Jodhpur Railway Station and
Airport, ensuring smooth and timely transportation.
•
Assisting artists during their stay, making sure that their needs and special requests were promptly and positively
addressed throughout the five-day event.
•
Serving as liaison support, ensuring seamless communication between the organizing committee and the artists.
•
Maintaining a strong volunteer presence across venues, contributing to the overall smooth execution of the festival.
The dedication, hospitality, and proactive efforts of the EBSB student team significantly enhanced the artist and guest 
experience, reflecting the spirit of national pride, cultural respect, and service that lies at the heart of the EBSB initiative.
The successful coordination and cultural exposure provided by the EBSB volunteers during Virasat enriched the festival’s 
impact and exemplified the values of unity, tradition, and teamwork. Their involvement added meaningful depth to the 
celebration of India’s diverse cultural heritage.

As per the provisions laid out in the Constitution of the Student Activity Council (SAC) and the Academic and 
Co-Curricular Activity Council (ACAC), the responsibility of organizing student activities both in offline and online 
platforms has been assigned to the President of the respective Boards under SAC and ACAC in FY 2024-25.
The Student Activity Council (SAC) comprises the following Boards: 
Board of Art & Culture
•
Board of Literary Affairs
•
Board of Student Sports
•
Board of Student Welfare
•
Board of Hostel Affairs
The Academic and Co-Curricular Activity Council (ACAC) consists of the following Boards:
•
Board of Departmental Societies
•
Board of Academic Interaction
•
Board of Innovation & Entrepreneurship
•
Board of Career Development
•
Board of Co-Curricular Affairs
•
Society of Alumni Affairs
These Boards, headed by their respective Presidents, are responsible for coordinating and facilitating various student 
activities within their designated domains. This allocation of responsibilities aims to ensure the smooth execution of student 
activities across both offline and online platforms, in accordance with the principles outlined in the Constitution of SAC and 
ACAC.

The Office of Training and Placement (T&P) at IIT Jodhpur plays a pivotal role in guiding students toward achieving their 
short-term and long-term career goals. It serves as a dedicated support system for students, helping them excel in their 
career paths through structured processes and personalized guidance.
A coordinated effort involving faculty members, staff, and active participation of student coordinators ensures that the 
career development plan remains effective and student centric. This plan includes assistance with internship opportunities, 
placement preparation, the application process, and final offer stages. Strategic support is provided to students at every step 
of their career planning journey.
The Office of T&P aspires to offer comprehensive career counselling to students not only during their academic tenure at
IIT Jodhpur but also after graduation. A range of services is offered including:
Training and Placement

Career development and planning

Competency and skill assessment

Professional and personal counselling

Informed decision-making support

Training in soft skills and interview preparedness
Through these initiatives, the Office of T&P fosters the development of essential professional skills, domain knowledge, and 
a positive attitude, enabling students to manage their careers with confidence and purpose.
The Placement Season 2024–25 was conducted in a hybrid mode, reflecting the evolving dynamics of recruitment 
processes. As of now, more than 200 reputed organizations have participated. These include:

Multinational Corporations (MNCs)

Core engineering and technology companies

Government and public sector undertakings (PSUs)

Startups and emerging ventures
The T&P Office continues to build and nurture symbiotic relationships with a wide network of industry leaders, IIT 
alumni, and governmental bodies. These relationships are maintained and strengthened through ongoing activities such as:

Social networking and alumni outreach

Industry workshops and seminars

Invited talks and lectures by professionals

Industrial visits and collaborative events
Through these consistent efforts, the Office of Training and Placement remains committed to enabling students of IIT 
Jodhpur to pursue meaningful and successful careers.
We at our institute witnessed over 200+ organisations rolling out close to 415+ offers to our students. Some of our 
prominent campus recruitment partners for this year has been Zomato, HCL Tech, ICICI Bank, CISCO, Microsoft, 
Google, TCS, Infosys, Ernst and Young, ZS Associates, Cognizant, Capgemini, DE Shaw, Arcesium, CDAC, Samsung, 
Accenture, Deloitte, B&Y Melon, Warner Brothers, Shaadi.com, MAQ, Reliance, Volvo Group, L&T, Royal Enfield, and 
Maruti Suzuki to name a few.
This year the T&P team had on-boarded new accounts such as ZS Associates, Capgemini, Cognizant, LTI Mindtree, 
MathWorks, Adverb, Morabu, PradhiAI, Hyundai Motors, Birla Group to name a few.
The roles and profiles offered to students during this placement season are a testament of the diversified and relevant 
courses offered at IIT Jodhpur. In addition, we have successfully built coherent relationships with our campus partners and 
strive to improve the students’ as well as the recruiters’ experience year after year. Office of Training & Placement has 
designed a curated capability programme to prepare students for the campus placement process. Throughout the year, the 
T&P Office at IIT Jodhpur organizes career development workshops, mock interviews, leadership talks, soft skill training 
and personality development activities.
